Emerging growth company <ix:nonNumeric contextRef="c-1" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt:fixed-false" id="f-22">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric> </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt;margin-top:2pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;&#9744; </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Item&#160;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On March&#160;21, 2024, Accenture plc (&#8220;Accenture&#8221;) issued a news release announcing financial results for its second quarter of fiscal 2024, which ended on February&#160;29, 2024.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A copy of the news release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99. All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:110%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Adjusted financial measures excluding the impact of business optimization costs and gain on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the business optimization costs and the investment gain facilitates an understanding as to the impact of these items and the company&#8217;s performance in comparison to the prior period. </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">(d)&#160;Exhibits</span></div><div $12.20</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; March&#160;21, 2024 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2024 ended February&#160;29, 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;In an uncertain macro environment, we remain the trusted partner to our clients for reinvention with a record 39 clients with quarterly bookings of over $100 million. We also extended our early lead in generative AI with $1.1 billion in new bookings in the first half of the year. And we are investing to serve the needs of our clients and expand our growth opportunities with $2.9 billion of capital deployed in the first half in strategic acquisitions. Thank you to our more than 740,000 people around the world for your dedication to delivering value for our clients.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues were $15.8 billion, and were flat in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared to the second quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income was $2.05 billion, compared to $1.94 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2023, and operating margin was 13.0% compared to 12.3% for the second quarter last year. Adjusted operating income was $2.16 billion, compared to $2.19 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2023 and adjusted operating margin was 13.7%, compared to 13.8% for the second quarter last year.</font></div><div style="margin-top:50pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted financial measures presented in this release are non-GAAP financial measures that exclude business optimization costs recorded in fiscal 2024 and fiscal 2023, as further described in this release.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted earnings per share were $2.63, an increase of 10% over $2.39 for the second quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted EPS were $2.77, an increase of 3% over $2.69 for the second quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the quarter were $21.6 billion, with consulting bookings of $10.5 billion and managed services bookings of $11.1 billion.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2024 were $15.80 billion, compared with $15.81 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2023, and were flat in both U.S. dollars and local currency growth. Revenues were slightly above the midpoint of the company's guided range of $15.40 billion to $16.00 billion. The foreign-exchange impact for the quarter was approximately negative 0.5%, which was consistent with the assumption provided in the company's first quarter earnings release.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $8.02 billion, a decrease of 3% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Managed Services revenues for the quarter were $7.78 billion, an increase of 3% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $2.63, a 10% increase over $2.39 for the second quarter of fiscal 2023. Excluding a $0.14 and $0.30 decrease for business optimization costs in the second quarter of fiscal 2024 and 2023, respectively, adjusted EPS were $2.77, a 3% increase over $2.69 last year. The $0.08 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.06 increase from higher non-operating income&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.06 increase from a lower effective tax rate&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">      partially offset by</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.03&#160;decrease from lower operating results&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01&#160;decrease from higher noncontrolling interests.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 30.9% compared to 30.6% in the second quarter of fiscal 2023. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the quarter were $2.72 billion, or 17.2% of revenues, compared with $2.65 billion, or 16.7% of revenues, for the second quarter of fiscal 2023.     </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income for the quarter increased 5%, to $2.05 billion, or 13.0% of revenues, compared with $1.94 billion, or 12.3% of revenues, for the second quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted operating income for the quarter was $2.16 billion, or 13.7% of revenues, compared with $2.19 billion, or 13.8% of revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company&#8217;s GAAP effective tax rate for the quarter was 18.4%, compared with 20.4% for the second quarter of fiscal 2023. The adjusted effective tax rate for the second quarter of fiscal 2024 was 18.8%, compared with 20.4% for the second quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP net income for the quarter was $1.71 billion, compared with $1.55 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted net income for the quarter was $1.80 billion, compared with $1.74 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $2.10 billion, and property and equipment additions were $110 million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $1.99 billion. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $2.33 billion&#59; property and equipment additions were $108 million&#59; and free cash flow was $2.22 billion.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 43 days at
